					if(e.layout==="fullscreen" || e.l==="fullscreen")
						newh = Math.max(e.mh,window.RSIH);
					else{
						e.gw = Array.isArray(e.gw) ? e.gw : [e.gw];

               </li>
               <li class="gdlr-core-skin-divider clearfix">
                <span class="gdlr-core-icon-list-icon-wrap gdlr-core-left">
                 <i class="gdlr-core-icon-list-icon fa fa-dot-circle-o">
                 </i>
                </span>
                <div class="gdlr-core-icon-list-content-wrap">
                 <span class="gdlr-core-icon-list-content">
                  Elementary level
                 </span>

             </div>

              <div class="gdlr-core-text-box-item-content" style="text-transform: none ;">
               <p>
                <strong>
                 Cost per level
                </strong>
                : KSH. 1,000.00 or 10USD application fee; Tuition fee KSH. 25,000.00 or 250USD
               </p>
               <p>
                <strong>
                 Duration of training
                </strong>
                : 3 months (equal to a semester) per level
               </p>
               <p>
                <strong>
                 Certification
                </strong>
                : A certificate of proficiency is issued to every successful candidate per level.
